# Smart AI Hub Metrics Dashboard

## Overview

**Last Updated:** October 15, 2025  
**Dashboard Refresh:** Real-time  
**Data Source:** Compliance Audit, Project Status, Progress Reports

This dashboard provides a visual representation of the Smart AI Hub project's progress, metrics, and key performance indicators. It offers at-a-glance insights into project health, completion status, and progress trends.

## Compliance Metrics
